<rate>1</rate><user>113642463191290398415<//user><Review>This store has great products, although incredibly expensive. They have so many pretty wrapping papers and stationary to wrap a gift beautifully.

I've been going to this store for a while and have always had overall pleasant experiences. But there's always a sense of arrogance from employees. I look young for my age and profession -I am a nurse- and am treated without a certain level of respect I see them give other customers. I will give them kudos for following decent safety  protocols, besides their staff VIOLATING people's personal space.

My brother visited the store for the first time and he was met with an even lower sense of respect- a sales associate snatched wrapping paper rolls out of hands. This is during a pandemic, mind you, so the violation of personal space is completely inexcusable. Also, she proceeded to ASK another customer if they wanted to have her take his wrapping paper rolls to the front. She then proceeded to follow my brother around the store, or perhaps the better word is stalking. The same sales associate came so close to us as we were browsing and led another customer through our path with no excuse or politeness. Their products are nice - albeit INCREDIBLY overpriced- but after this experience, they no longer have my business. I'm a COVID ICU RN and I'll be damned if I spend anymore of my hard earned cash at such a deplorable place.

*When calling the manager the next day, he was incredibly dismissive and essentially pushed my complaint aside. The products are great, the staff is disreputable. They racially profile, serve certain customers better than others, and lack any care when they're called out for it. Go somewhere else!< /Review><Date>1607825413676<//Date></record></dataset><record>

<Text>I dropped my friend off at this place so that she could do her laundry for free. They also have free bathrooms, showers 24 hours a day.

And if you go between 7AM and 7PM they allow you to do 1 load of your laundry and let you use their charging stations for your electronics.

Its amazing places like this exist.  I only used the bathroom and charged my phone while I waited for her to do her laundry.

They also take donations, I gave them a couple bags of clothes and hygiene items and they were very grateful.

While I waited, I watched this amazing artist freehand draw the most incredible piece of art, just breath taking work!

This place is located in skid row and the area looks intimidating but the people that go there and the employees are good people.<//Text><username>Maggie Bakhtiari< /username><user_id>116291639814743446061</user_id>< Rating>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
I made a google account just so I could leave this review .
Ricardo and his associates were friendly, laidback, and non pushy yet totally professional .
I knew what vehicle I was interested in from looking on their website the night before . I was handed a key and told to take my time and check it out and they would answer any questions I had.
They brought me the car fax to look over and once I decided the car was what I really wanted - Ricardo made the whole transition as smooth as possible. He was able to get my monthly payments to what I was comfortable with. He took the time to explain everything to me, answered everything I asked and was just totally upfront.
I told him I would have to drive my old car back home and would Uber it back to the dealership. He said there was no need to use a Uber- that one of the guys could follow me home if I was okay to bring them back . ( Of course I was happy to do that )
Eli was the gentleman who safely drove my car home and when I took him back , we had a nice cordial conversation.
As I was about to drop him off - I noticed I had a small tiny crack towards the bottom of my front windshield. I am not sure if a small rock had hit it , or I had just overlooked it - but they were quick to send me to the windshield guy across the street ( I think his name was Marco- who happened to also be really nice and did a great job ) Plus Car Depot paid for the repair !
Great customer service like this is hard to come by. I was treated fairly and respectful AND got a reliable , well maintained and great cute little car!
Thank you Car Depot , Ricardo,
Eli and the rest of the team ! I was so glad none of you were creepy , cheesy car salesmen!  ;)
I highly recommend  you over and over.<//review>

My fiance and I bought a 2015 Nissan Altima SV from Car Depot today! It was in great condition and we'd typically have our mechanic give it the all clear, but there were no red flags after our own thorough check and we were sold!

My fiance just loves the size and comfort of the Nissan Altima so that's all we've been looking for for weeks and Car Depot offered a great deal on this one, which had been on the lot for just about 3 months.

Mike answered the phone when we called today to confirm the car was still available; he was very friendly, knowledgeable, transparent, and helped us through the entire process - answered our questions as we inspected the car, went on a test drive, and promptly worked with his team to ensure the minor issues we uncovered were addressed or looked into (the power steering fluid was nearly out, there were weird seemingly spilled beverage marks/stains on the media center, and does the car have one or two key fobs? - unfortunately only one). The Nissan had clearly been well taken care of and prepared for sale and we were not about to pass this up!  From the initial inspection through the test drive and purchase/paperwork, we spent about 3.5 or 4 hours there before leaving with our new-to-us car - not bad!

We were offered three different extended warranty packages offered by Alpha Warranty Services each at different prices/tiers, declined, and were offered a discount on the recommended one and still declined. Alpha has great reviews on Google but a lot of recent, really concerning reviews on Yelp and we just didn't think we'd get our money's worth for shelling out another $1.5-3k on that alone. We are very pleased with Car Depot's included 30-day warranty package though, which covers 50% or more of the cost of any engine or transmission issues.

< text>
I have been shopping here for the past year. The staff has always been friendly; and although it is a bit more expensive to get vape cartridges and juice here than other shops. It is near my house and that is the price of convenience.

However, I recently had a bad set of cartridges for my juul and came back a couple hours later, and it turns out they do not offer exchanges. When I opened the package the first cartridge was not hitting properly and I removed it and it leaked juice all over the place, I opened and inspected two more and they were leaking as well.

It is not good business practice to make the customer bite the bullet for a bad product. They charge $20 dollars for the pack cartridges which is one third more expensive than you can buy them for online. Which I was okay with paying for in a pinch. Sadly, I won't be shopping here anymore and will either shop online or make the drive to some of the other shops that I know who will honor exchanges for damaged products.

I would highly suggest the owner changes his policies on this.< /text>

Poway smoke shop is wonderful. Seeing such a variety of cigars and cigarillos all in a massive cedar walk in humidor made my day. The wide selection was slightly over priced, but is worth it for the quality. Perfectly kept cigars. A nice collection of glass water pipes, and hookahs, the water pipes may appear over priced, but is because most are hand blown locally by a quality artist. Examine the pieces and you'll notice most are thick and strong, well balanced between function and aesthetics. Dont complain about a credit surcharge, their common, just hit up an ATM before you go! Friendly owner, talked to him for nearly 20 minutes about his humidor and shop. Recommend this smoke shop for Hookahs, glass, and cigars, but not for rolling tobacco, papers or lighters, grab them from your local gas station.</Text>

I'd give it five stars it's the pricing was more fair or if they could at least match vapordna price. That seems reasonable to me I mean I'm not going to price match to eBay or some random Chinese site or whatever but vapordna seems to be the giant online vabe store that they are competing with.<//Review>

< Text>
The selection is great among all relevant smokeshop product categories, though their vape selection is almost entirely made up of this fragile generation of smok.  The employees actually vape and know at least something about the products-an extreme rarity among the dozens of smoke and vape shops I've been to.
